<script>
	function header_regions_load() {
		$.ajax({
			type: "GET",
			async: false,
			url: 'https://images.elecity.ru/shared_data_template/ajax/ajax.php?act=header_regions_table&request_uri=L3NlYXJjaC8/cT1wb2xhcmlzJiZwPTE=',
			success: function(data) {
				$('#change_cur_region .modal-body').html(data);
			}
		});

		$('#change_cur_region').modal('toggle');
	}

	function ask_region_show() {
		$('#geoip-popup').fadeIn();
	}
	function ask_region_hide() {
		$('#geoip-popup').hide();
	}
	function ask_region_save() {
		localStorage.setItem('ask_region_hide', 'true');
	}	

	$(function() {
		$(document).on("click","#ask_region_no",function() {
			ask_region_hide();
			header_regions_load();
		});

		//При клике на город, больше не вызываем вопрос о городе
		$(document).on("click","#change_cur_region .modal-body a",function() {
			ask_region_save();
		});		

		//кнопка ДА
		$(document).on("click","#ask_region_yes",function() {
			ask_region_save();
			ask_region_hide();

			if($(this).data("goto")!='' ){
				if(location.host != $(this).data("goto") )//Делаем переход только если текущий домен не совпадает с нужным
					location.href='https://'+$(this).data("goto");
				else location.reload();
			}else location.reload();

		});	
		//вызываем вопрос о городе если пользователь зашел впервые или не выбрал город
			});
</script>
<div class="col-xlg-3 col-lg-3 col-md-3 col-sm-4 col-xs-5 nopadding">

<script>
(function($) {
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var $header = $("header"),
            $clone = $header.before($header.clone().addClass("clone"));

        $(window).on("scroll", function() {
            var fromTop = $(document).scrollTop();
            $("body").toggleClass("down", (fromTop > 200));
        });
    });
})(jQuery);


</script>

<script>
	jQuery(function($) {


		if (jQuery('.shortcode-toggle').length) {
			jQuery('.shortcode-toggle').each(function() {
				var toggleObj = jQuery(this);
				toggleObj.closedText = toggleObj.find('input[name="title_closed"]').attr('value');
				toggleObj.openText = toggleObj.find('input[name="title_open"]').attr('value');
				// Add logic for the optional excerpt text.
				if (toggleObj.find('a.more-link.read-more').length) {
					toggleObj.readMoreText = toggleObj.find('a.more-link.read-more').text();
					toggleObj.readLessText = toggleObj.find('a.more-link.read-more').attr('readless');
					toggleObj.find('a.more-link.read-more').removeAttr('readless');
					toggleObj.find('a.more-link').click(function() {
						var moreTextObj = jQuery(this).next('.more-text');
						moreTextObj.animate({
							opacity: 'toggle',							height: 'toggle'
						}, 300).css('display', 'block');
						moreTextObj.toggleClass('open').toggleClass('closed');
						if (moreTextObj.hasClass('open')) {
							jQuery(this).text(toggleObj.readLessText);
						} // End IF Statement
						if (moreTextObj.hasClass('closed')) {
							jQuery(this).text(toggleObj.readMoreText);
						} // End IF Statement
						return false;
					});
				}
				toggleObj.find('input[name="title_closed"]').remove();
				toggleObj.find('input[name="title_open"]').remove();
				toggleObj.find('span.toggle-trigger a').click(function() {
					toggleObj.find('.toggle-content').animate({
						opacity: 'toggle',						height: 'toggle'
					}, 300);
					toggleObj.toggleClass('open').toggleClass('closed');
					if (toggleObj.hasClass('open')) {
						jQuery(this).text(toggleObj.openText);
					} // End IF Statement
					if (toggleObj.hasClass('closed')) {
						jQuery(this).text(toggleObj.closedText);
					} // End IF Statement
					return false;
				});
			});
		} // End IF Statement
	}); // jQuery()
</script>

<script>
	window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
	function gtm_product_click(list, id, name, price, brand, product_position, category_name)
	{
		dataLayer.push({
			event: 'gtm-ee-event',
			'gtm-ee-event-category': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
			'gtm-ee-event-action': 'Product Clicks',
			'gtm-ee-event-non-interaction': 'False',
			ecommerce: {
				click: {
					actionField: {
						list: 'List 1'
					},
					products: [{
						id: id,
						name: name,
						price: price,
						brand: brand,
						category: category_name,
						position: product_position,
						variant: '-'
					}]
				}
			}
		});

		dataLayer.push({
			event: 'productClick',
			ecommerce: {
				click: {
					actionField: {
						list: 'Товары'
					},
					products: [{
						id: id,
						name: name,
						price: price,
						brand: brand,
						category: category_name,
						position: product_position
					}]
				}
			}
		});

	}
	function gtm_add_to_cart_click(list, id, name, price, brand, category_name, quantity)
	{
		if (!quantity)
		{
			quantity = $('body .add-to-cart-count').val();
		}

		dataLayer.push({
			event: 'gtm-ee-event',
			'gtm-ee-event-category': 'Enhanced Ecommerce',
			'gtm-ee-event-action': 'Adding a Product to a Shopping Cart',
			'gtm-ee-event-non-interaction': 'False',
			ecommerce: {
				add: {
					products: [{
						name: name,
						id: id,
						price: price,
						brand: brand,
						category: category_name,
						variant: '',
						quantity: quantity
					}]
				}
			}
		});
		dataLayer.push({
			event: 'addToCart',
			ecommerce: {
				add: {
					actionField: {
						list: 'Товары'
					},
					products: [{
						name: name,
						id: id,
						price: price,
						brand: brand,
						category: category_name,
						variant: '',
						quantity: quantity
					}]
				}
			}
		});
		
		gtag('event', 'add_to_cart', {
			'send_to': 'AW-587089971',
			'value': price,
			'items': [{
			  'id': id,
			  'google_business_vertical': 'retail'
			}]
		  });
	}
</script>
<script>


$( window ).load(function() {

	if($("[data-style]").length){

		$("[data-style]").each(function(){
			$(this).parent().html($(this).parent().html().replace('data-style', 'style'));
		})

	}

	if($(".item [data-src]").length){ 

		$(".item [data-src]").each(function(){

			$(this).parent().html($(this).parent().html().replace('data-src', 'src'));

		});

	}

});

</script>

<script>
$( document ).on( "click", ".catalog_item_column_3_zag", function(){
	if($(this).find(".triangle_close").length){
		var el = $(this).find(".triangle_close");
		el.removeClass('triangle_close');
		el.addClass('triangle_open');
			/*$(this).parent().parent().find('.catalog_item_column_3_text').fadeIn();*/
		$(this).parents('.catalog_item_column_3_block').find('.catalog_item_column_3_text').fadeIn();	
	}
	else if($(this).find(".triangle_open").length){
		var el = $(this).find(".triangle_open");
		el.removeClass('triangle_open');
		el.addClass('triangle_close');
			/*$(this).parent().parent().find('.catalog_item_column_3_text').fadeIn();*/
		$(this).parents('.catalog_item_column_3_block').find('.catalog_item_column_3_text').fadeOut();
	}
					
});
</script>
